## Opcodes

```
  0: 0x0001 [0x03] ExtData[1]->WorkLocal[0] = 1*
  1: 0x0006 [0x03] ExtData[1]->WorkLocal[3] = 0*
  2: 0x000B [0x03] ExtData[1]->WorkLocal[17] = 0*
  3: 0x0010 [0x03] ExtData[1]->WorkLocal[13] = 0*
  4: 0x0015 [0x03] ExtData[1]->WorkLocal[12] = 0*
```
